<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plechtig.html>plechtig</a> (11930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">plichtich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">plechtich</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:plicht.html>plicht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-ig</i>.
